## ======== Risk parity strategy ======== ##

# Clear workspace

rm(list=ls()) ; par(mfrow=c(1,1))
library(xts)
library(zoo)
library(nloptr)


# Import daily returns to build volatilty measure

dret <- read.csv("U:/R/dret.csv")
sd.narm <- function(x) sd(x, na.rm=T)

h <- 60 # days to estimate volatility

dvols <- rollapply(dret[,2:ncol(dret)], h, sd.narm)
dvols <- data.frame(dret$Date[h:nrow(dret)], dvols)
colnames(dvols)[1] <- "Date"
dvols$Date <- as.Date(dvols$Date,"%d/%m/%Y")


# Creating initial weights

dret.wod <- dret[,-1]
dvols.wod <- dvols[,-1]

w <- NULL
w <- as.data.frame(w)

for (k in 1:ncol(dvols.wod)){ # for k assets
  for (i in 1:nrow(dvols.wod)){ # for n months
    w[i,k] <- 1/(dvols.wod[i,k]*sqrt(261))
  }
}

w <- as.matrix(w)
w <- w[32:6107,]


# Rolling covariance matrix

c <- 90 # 90 days to estimate covariance matrix

dret$Date <- as.Date(dret$Date, "%d/%m/%Y")
dret.wod <- dret[,-1]

date.list <- read.csv("U:/R/date.list.csv")
date.list <- as.matrix(date.list)

rcov1 = function(i) cov(dret.wod[i:(i+c),1:8],use="pairwise.complete.obs")
rcov2 = function(i) cov(dret.wod[i:(i+c),9:17],use="pairwise.complete.obs")
rcov3 = function(i) cov(dret.wod[i:(i+c),18:22],use="pairwise.complete.obs")
rcov4 = function(i) cov(dret.wod[i:(i+c),23:31],use="pairwise.complete.obs")
rcov5 = function(i) cov(dret.wod[i:(i+c),32:36],use="pairwise.complete.obs")


# === Optimisation === #

## EQUITY

# Objective function
f <- function(w) {
  return(-(log(w[1])+log(w[2])+log(w[3])+log(w[4])+log(w[5])+log(w[6])+log(w[7])+log(w[8])))
}

# Gradient of the objective function
grad.f <- function(w) {
  return(c(-1/w[1],-1/w[2],-1/w[3],-1/w[4],-1/w[5],-1/w[6],-1/w[7],-1/w[8]))
}

# Risk constraint
risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return(as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:8])%*%rcov1(i)%*%cbind(w[1:8])))-0.14)
  }
}

# Gradient of the risk constraint
grad.risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return((rcov1(i)%*%cbind(w[1:8]))/as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:8])%*%rcov1(i)%*%cbind(w[1:8]))))
  }
}

# Solving the minimisation function
weights = function(i) {
  rpw <- nloptr(x0=w[i,1:8],
                eval_f=f,
                eval_grad_f=grad.f,
                eval_g_eq=risk.const(i),
                eval_jac_g_eq=grad.risk.const(i),
                lb=c(rep(0,8)),
                opts=list("algorithm"="NLOPT_LD_SLSQP","xtol_rel"=1.0e-8))
  return(as.matrix(rpw$solution))
}

rpwieq <- as.data.frame(rpwieq)

                  weights(6070),weights(6071),weights(6072),weights(6073),weights(6074),weights(6075),weights(6076)))

write.csv(rpwieq,"U:/R/rpwieq.csv")


## FIXED INCOME

# Objective function
f <- function(w) {
  return(-(log(w[1])+log(w[2])+log(w[3])+log(w[4])+log(w[5])+log(w[6])+log(w[7])+log(w[8])+log(w[9])))
}

# Gradient of the objective function
grad.f <- function(w) {
  return(c(-1/w[1],-1/w[2],-1/w[3],-1/w[4],-1/w[5],-1/w[6],-1/w[7],-1/w[8],-1/w[9]))
}

# Risk constraint
risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return(as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:9])%*%rcov2(i)%*%cbind(w[1:9])))-0.14)
  }
}

# Gradient of the risk constraint
grad.risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return((rcov2(i)%*%cbind(w[1:9]))/as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:9])%*%rcov2(i)%*%cbind(w[1:9]))))
  }
}

# Solving the minimisation function
weights = function(i) {
  rpw <- nloptr(x0=w[i,9:17],
                eval_f=f,
                eval_grad_f=grad.f,
                eval_g_eq=risk.const(i),
                eval_jac_g_eq=grad.risk.const(i),
                lb=c(rep(0,9)),
                opts=list("algorithm"="NLOPT_LD_SLSQP","xtol_rel"=1.0e-8))
  return(as.matrix(rpw$solution))
}

rpwifi <- NULL
rpwifi <- as.data.frame(rpwifi)

## CURRENCY

# Objective function
f <- function(w) {
  return(-(log(w[1])+log(w[2])+log(w[3])+log(w[4])+log(w[5])))
}

# Gradient of the objective function
grad.f <- function(w) {
  return(c(-1/w[1],-1/w[2],-1/w[3],-1/w[4],-1/w[5]))
}

# Risk constraint
risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return(as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:5])%*%rcov3(i)%*%cbind(w[1:5])))-0.14)
  }
}

# Gradient of the risk constraint
grad.risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return((rcov3(i)%*%cbind(w[1:5]))/as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:5])%*%rcov3(i)%*%cbind(w[1:5]))))
  }
}

# Solving the minimisation function
weights = function(i) {
  rpw <- nloptr(x0=w[i,18:22],
                eval_f=f,
                eval_grad_f=grad.f,
                eval_g_eq=risk.const(i),
                eval_jac_g_eq=grad.risk.const(i),
                lb=c(rep(0,5)),
                opts=list("algorithm"="NLOPT_LD_SLSQP","xtol_rel"=1.0e-8))
  return(as.matrix(rpw$solution))
}

## COMMODITY

# Objective function
f <- function(w) {
  return(-(log(w[1])+log(w[2])+log(w[3])+log(w[4])+log(w[5])+log(w[6])+log(w[7])+log(w[8])+log(w[9])))
}

# Gradient of the objective function
grad.f <- function(w) {
  return(c(-1/w[1],-1/w[2],-1/w[3],-1/w[4],-1/w[5],-1/w[6],-1/w[7],-1/w[8],-1/w[9]))
}

# Risk constraint
risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return(as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:9])%*%rcov4(i)%*%cbind(w[1:9])))-0.14)
  }
}

# Gradient of the risk constraint
grad.risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return((rcov4(i)%*%cbind(w[1:9]))/as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:9])%*%rcov4(i)%*%cbind(w[1:9]))))
  }
}

# Solving the minimisation function
weights = function(i) {
  rpw <- nloptr(x0=w[i,23:31],
                eval_f=f,
                eval_grad_f=grad.f,
                eval_g_eq=risk.const(i),
                eval_jac_g_eq=grad.risk.const(i),
                lb=c(rep(0,9)),
                opts=list("algorithm"="NLOPT_LD_SLSQP","xtol_rel"=1.0e-8))
  return(as.matrix(rpw$solution))
}

rpwicmdty <- NULL
rpwicmdty <- as.data.frame(rpwicmdty)

                     weights(50),weights(51),weights(52),weights(53),weights(54),weights(55),weights(56),weights(57),weights(58),weights(59),
                     weights(60),weights(61),weights(62),weights(63),weights(64),weights(65),weights(66),weights(67),weights(68),weights(69),
                     weights(70),weights(71),weights(72),weights(73),weights(74),weights(75),weights(76),weights(77),weights(78),weights(79),

## ENERGY

# Objective function
f <- function(w) {
  return(-(log(w[1])+log(w[2])+log(w[3])+log(w[4])+log(w[5])))
}

# Gradient of the objective function
grad.f <- function(w) {
  return(c(-1/w[1],-1/w[2],-1/w[3],-1/w[4],-1/w[5]))
}

# Risk constraint
risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return(as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:5])%*%rcov5(i)%*%cbind(w[1:5])))-0.14)
  }
}

# Gradient of the risk constraint
grad.risk.const <- function(i) {
  function(w) {
    return((rcov5(i)%*%cbind(w[1:5]))/as.numeric(sqrt(rbind(w[1:5])%*%rcov5(i)%*%cbind(w[1:5]))))
  }
}

# Solving the minimisation function
weights = function(i) {
  rpw <- nloptr(x0=w[i,32:36],
                eval_f=f,
                eval_grad_f=grad.f,
                eval_g_eq=risk.const(i),
                eval_jac_g_eq=grad.risk.const(i),
                lb=c(rep(0,5)),
                opts=list("algorithm"="NLOPT_LD_SLSQP","xtol_rel"=1.0e-8))
  return(as.matrix(rpw$solution))
}

rpwinrg <- NULL
rpwinrg <- as.data.frame(rpwinrg)
